Central and National Government Weekly Memorial Services

▲Central Party Headquarters: At 9:00 a.m. on the 13th, the Central Party Headquarters held the Weekly Memorial Service for the Premier. Sun Ke, Liu Luyin, Ma Chaojun, Yu Jingtang, Liu Jiwen, Gui Chongji, Chen Lifu, Zhang Qun, Cheng Tianfang, and hundreds of officials from various departments and committees attended. Sun Ke presided, and Liu Jiwen reported on the general situation of party affairs in Shandong, stating briefly that party affairs in Shandong began to be organized separately after the suppression of the rebellion. The party and government are in harmony, with a total of 5,400 party members. Among the 108 counties in the province, formal county party headquarters have been established in 14 counties, including Pingyuan. Those under reorganization include 69 counties, including Weixian. Nine counties, including Qufu, have established preparatory committees for directly affiliated district party headquarters. Four counties, including Boping, have established preparatory committees for directly affiliated district sub-headquarters. Special party commissioners have been dispatched to ten counties, including Jiyang County. Other counties have established preparatory committees or publicity officers for county party headquarters. Various counties do not pay much attention to publicity and training. The organization of mass organizations is loose, but funding is sufficient. After the takeover of Weihaiwei, a party headquarters was immediately established, and there are now more than 30 party members. The directly affiliated district party headquarters and mass organizations have also been organized and established. The Jiaoji Railway Special Party Headquarters has 264 party members, divided into three district party headquarters. The important task is to strictly prevent reactionary elements and publications. The Qingdao City Party has more than 350 party members and more than 900 probationary party members. The city is divided into six district party headquarters and one directly affiliated district sub-headquarters. The organization, publicity, and training have all been successful. Social organizations have all been organized, and the party and government are also cooperating, with no difficulties in funding. Most of the new party members are workers, followed by students. There is little activity, but reactionary publications have not disappeared. The meeting then adjourned.

▲National Government: At 10:00 a.m. on the same day, the National Government held the Weekly Memorial Service for the Premier. Yu Youren, Wang Chonghui, Shao Yuanchong, Niu Yongjian, Wang Boqun, Ru Yuli, Song Ziwen, Ma Fuxiang, He Yaozu, Wang Zhengting, and staff from the two offices of civil affairs and military affairs, totaling more than 300 people, attended. Wang Chonghui presided, and Shao Yuanchong spoke about the mission of the nation, stating briefly that the mission of the nation has three aspects: (1) To protect the people, resist foreign aggression, and maintain social stability. (2) To nurture the people, so that all people can thrive under the principles of joint production and joint consumption. (3) To educate the people, so that everyone has the opportunity to receive education, so that they can exert their greatest efforts to seek social progress. China's international status is still unequal, and the powers still treat us with the attitude of the strong towards the weak. They do not know that the unlimited evolution of mankind comes from lasting international peace, and peace depends on mutual respect between nations. The ceremony then adjourned.

Wang Zhengting

Report at the Weekly Memorial Service of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs

▲After the Abolition of Consular Jurisdiction

▲Attitude That Chinese People Should Take Toward Foreigners

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs held the Weekly Memorial Service for the Premier on the 13th. Chairman Wang Zhengting reported on the attitude that Chinese people should take toward foreigners after the abolition of consular jurisdiction, stating briefly that the biggest obstacle to abolishing unequal treaties is consular jurisdiction. Now that the date of abolition is not far off, we should pay attention to what attitude the Chinese people should take toward foreigners after abolition. Chinese and foreign customs, languages, etiquette, and various other things are different, so misunderstandings and disputes easily arise. China is a country of etiquette, and treats people with courtesy in all interactions. During the Qin Shi Huang and Yuan Ming Dynasties, foreigners came to China to travel and were treated favorably by the Chinese government. In the eighteenth century, when maritime restrictions were greatly relaxed, the number of foreigners coming to China increased greatly. The motives of most of them, except for a few who were well-intentioned, were to seize the interests of our country. Since foreigners adopted this attitude towards China, conflicts arose from time to time. Lin Wenzhong's burning of opium was extremely reasonable, but foreign countries unreasonably interfered, leading to the Opium War. China concluded a treaty after being defeated, which was the beginning of China losing territory. Later, various countries followed suit and demanded the same, and concessions and leased territories continued to be established. By the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895, China was defeated again, and its weaknesses were fully exposed. The countries then became even more reckless, and China was trapped under the heavy pressure of unequal treaties. Since China was conquered by foreign countries, foreigners in China became even more reckless, which led to the Boxer Rebellion. The change in the Chinese people's attitude towards foreigners, from friendship to hostility, was not the fault of the Chinese. Now that the time for the abolition of consular jurisdiction is approaching, should the Chinese people harbor a desire for revenge against foreigners after consular jurisdiction is abolished? This is fundamentally wrong. Our country has always been a country of etiquette, and will never take revenge on foreigners. Foreigners residing in China are guests from China's point of view, so Chinese people should treat them with the courtesy of guests. However, foreigners must obey Chinese laws and fulfill the same obligations as Chinese citizens. In the past, the Manchu Qing government, unwilling to have relations with foreigners, deliberately demarcated certain areas as foreign settlements. For the sake of convenience, everything within these settlements was left unattended, gradually leading to guests acting as hosts and the loss of sovereignty. Now, the Chinese people are aware of the drawbacks and unanimously demand the return of the concessions. Consular jurisdiction will soon be resolved, and the second step is to proceed with the return of concessions and leased territories. Chinese people have the right to live freely in foreign countries, so China should grant foreigners the right to live freely after it reclaims the concessions and leased territories. However, this right should only be granted after the concessions and leased territories have been completely reclaimed and foreign troops and warships have been completely withdrawn. It should also be subject to appropriate restrictions, following the precedent of various countries. From now on, interactions between Chinese and foreigners should be based on a spirit of mutual equality, so that foreigners will have no excuse to complain. The nation should pay attention to this point.

President Chiang

Participates in the Zhejiang Provincial Joint Memorial Week

▲Advocates Using China's Inherent Morality and Peace

▲To Achieve the Goal of Abolishing Unequal Treaties

The Zhejiang Provincial Party, Government, Military, and Police agencies held a joint Weekly Memorial Service for the Premier at the Provincial Party Headquarters at 9:00 a.m. today (the 13th). Party and government officials and staff from all sides, totaling about 2,000 people, attended. President Chiang arrived at about 9:00 a.m., and the ceremony began immediately. President Chiang presided. After a moment of silence, President Chiang lectured on the Premier's teachings, stating briefly that he had spoken here the day before, and that the focus of the National Assembly was on the Provisional Constitution and the abolition of unequal treaties. It must be known that this meeting is the key to China's survival, and all citizens should contribute their knowledge and ability. Speaking to this point, he read a section on the conclusion of nationalism from the booklet he was holding, saying that it could be seen from this that the Premier had instructed us to restore the position of the Chinese nation, and that it should be based on China's inherent morality and peace. Therefore, the abolition of unequal treaties should not rely on the courage of a single person in three or five minutes, nor should it adopt the xenophobic methods of the Boxers, which would only increase various obstacles and suffering. Now, the imperialists, seeing that the foundation of the Chinese revolution is gradually becoming consolidated, have tacitly formed a united front. Under these circumstances, we must seek survival from death, fight together, and diligently fulfill our duties with strong, persevering, and enduring spirit, and bury ourselves in hard work. Only then can we succeed. Since the Tang and Song Dynasties, China has been bullied by foreign tribes, and has recovered its national position with this spirit. Moreover, there are good examples in Zhejiang. In the past, King Goujian of Yue spent ten years accumulating resources and ten years teaching his people, and persevered through hardship, eventually achieving his goals. Although our country's position is now extremely difficult, if everyone can become self-reliant, it will not take ten years. As long as we are willing to work hard, without having to sleep on firewood and taste gall, we can abolish unequal treaties and restore the nation's position. If we give up on ourselves, we will be letting ourselves down. After this National Assembly, we will see which country is willing to give up unequal treaties, and that country will be our friend. The ceremony adjourned at 10:00 a.m.

Labor and Police Unrest at Zichuan Coal Mine

Jitong Correspondence: At the Zichuan Coal Mine of the Shandong Luda Company, a misunderstanding arose due to the mine police inspecting for smuggled coal, resulting in a conflict between the workers and the police. The mine police station arrested three workers. When the workers' demand for their release was not met, they destroyed the mine police station, resulting in a major unrest. The labor union demanded that the mine police apologize for firing without authorization. The mine police also demanded that the workers be punished. The two sides were deadlocked. The Department of Agriculture and Mines and the Provincial Party Headquarters sent personnel to mediate, but the matter has not been resolved. Details are as follows:

▲Cause of the Incident: On the 27th of last month, workers Li Hezheng, Li Changxi, and Liu Zhahe from the Dakunlun branch mine of Zichuan were transporting waste rocks from the mine when they encountered guard mine police Tu Xiangliang inspecting for smuggled coal. A verbal dispute arose, resulting in a conflict. Li Changxi and the other two were arrested by the mine police station at the mine. When the Dakunlun labor union heard about this, it immediately sent representatives Guo Yunkun to the station to demand their release. Workers followed and inquired along the way, and more and more gathered. When they arrived in front of the police station, there were already hundreds of people. When Wu Zhensheng, the squad leader, saw the large group of workers approaching, he ordered the gate to be closed tightly. At this time, with so many people and diverse opinions, order was lost. They climbed the windows and knocked on the doors, making a great commotion. Some of the workers held sticks and stones to knock on the door. One person took the lead, and the others followed suit. The mine police inside did not know the situation outside, but only saw the windows broken and the doors torn, and stones hitting them. They fired shots into the air to stop them. At this time, the workers outside were pushing forward and backward, breaking down the door and entering. The mine police who had guns were afraid to fire them, and instead held the butt of the guns to resist. There was a chaotic scene, with bowls, cups, bedding, and mattresses thrown all over the ground. More than ten mine police officers fled out the door, and the workers triumphantly carried out the three who had been arrested. Afterwards, the mine police station inspected the damage and found three rifles damaged and two pistols missing. They immediately reported this by telephone to the mine police station. Deputy Director Huang Liyuan rushed to the scene after hearing the report, but the workers had already dispersed. Only Guo Yunkun and Liu Zhahe were captured within the mine. Li Changxi was arrested near the mine by the mine police who were on the scene. Soon after, labor union director Li Wencheng and others also rushed to the scene after hearing the news and had a verbal conflict with Huang Liyuan. Li rebuked Huang for not notifying the labor union, for not punishing the mine police for firing without authorization, and for re-arresting the workers. Huang said that the workers destroyed the police station and smashed the guns, so they should be arrested and investigated. The mine police fired into the air as an emergency measure. Both sides were angry and unwilling to yield. Huang then photographed the damage to the station and reported it to the company and the Zichuan County Office. Li also reported the firing by the mine police and the arrest of the three workers to the labor union for negotiations, and notified the County Party Headquarters.

▲Mediation Process: On the 28th, Yang Suwu, the manager of the Luda Company, arrived at the mine. Zichuan County Chief Meng Guanglu, together with the Public Security Bureau Chief and the County Party Headquarters Committee members, went to the scene of the incident for inspection. Then, they convened the Chinese manager of the Luda Company, Yang Suwu, the Japanese manager Song Xiang, the labor union directors Gu Chi and Li Wencheng, and others at the Coal Mine Club for preliminary mediation. The company and the mine police station demanded that the workers involved in the incident be punished according to law, that the lost guns be recovered, and questioned the labor union about its powers beyond those stipulated in the Labor Union Law. The labor union, on the other hand, demanded that the director of the mine police station, Huang Liyuan, and the mine police be punished for firing without authorization, and that the mine police apologize to the arrested workers and the company apologize to the labor union. The two sides were at extreme ends and could not reach an agreement. Huang immediately asked the County Chief to take the three arrested

Page 7

Continued Important News

people back and detain them for punishment. The County Public Security Bureau Chief, because the three had already been detained at the mine police station for one night, and fearing that there might be torture, refused to take them back. He required the mine police station to officially send a letter to the county. In the afternoon, after the mine police station sent the three to the county, they were immediately bailed out by the County Party Headquarters and the Tiger Society. Because mediation was hopeless, the labor union immediately reported to the Provincial Party Headquarters, and the company also reported to the Department of Agriculture and Mines for review. On the 30th, Bureau Chief Liu of the Mining Bureau arrived at the mine. On the 31st, Lieutenant Colonel Lu of the Boshan Army High Regiment, Committee Member Li of the Provincial Party Headquarters, and Committee Member Gu Wenlin of the Department of Agriculture and Mines all arrived at the mine. They thoroughly investigated the facts of the incident on one hand, and engaged in mediation on the other hand. It was heard that the mediation conditions were that both the mine police and the workers would be released without being questioned, that the company would pay wages and medical expenses to workers who stopped work and were injured, and that the workers involved in the incident who disobeyed inspection and destroyed the mine police station should submit a letter of repentance to the company to express their remorse. Later, because the company was rewarding riots for the two items of suspended wages and injury costs, it refused to accept, while the labor union insisted that the mine police should apologize to the labor union. The distance between the two sides is still far, and it has not been resolved. It is now heard that the committee members sent by the province have reported the investigation and mediation situation to the Department of Agriculture and Mines and the Provincial Party Headquarters in detail. The Department of Agriculture and Mines has also formulated considerable measures for this matter, and it is expected to be resolved soon. (April 10th)

Internal Division of the Red Bandits in Western Fujian

▲Stalin Faction Massacres Social Democrats

▲Deng Zihui and Fu Bocui Slaughter Each Other

Shantou Correspondence: After Zhang Zhen's division recovered the bandit dens in Kan City and Hulei in Yongding, Fujian Province, the Red Bandit Twelfth Army under Deng Zihui fled into the mountains. Yesterday, Zhang's division sent a victory telegram, stating that on the morning of March 28, the Red Bandits attacked Kan City, but were jointly attacked by the Yongding military police and local militia, resulting in the capture of 32 Communist bandits and the killing of over a hundred bandits. They seized 15 Mauser pistols, 65 rain capes, and 70 7.9mm rifles. The captured bandits were interrogated by Brigade Commander Wang and executed on the spot. Over ten heads were displayed in the Badun and Paitanzi Jiao areas. Furthermore, according to individuals from Yongding who came to Shantou, the Red Bandits in Western Fujian have experienced extreme divisions in the past three months. After Zhang's division recovered Longyan and Yongding, many local Communists successively repented and surrendered. According to reports from those who had reformed, the internal conflicts of the Red Bandits had escalated from divisions to mutual killings. Previously, the three counties of Shanghang, Longyan, and Yongding were held as strongholds by the Communist bandits, who possessed significant power. They established the pseudo-Soviet government of Western Fujian, directly under the command of the Third International. The party leaders included Guo Diren, Lin Yizhu, Fu Bocui, Deng Zihui, Zhang Dingcheng, Lu Zhaoxi, and Wei Wu, among others. However, these individuals harbored different ambitions. There was a division between the Stalinist cadres and the Trotskyist social democrats. Deng Zihui belonged to the Stalinist faction, centered around the Soviet Red Army in Western Fujian, while Guo Diren belonged to the Trotskyist faction, centered around the Red Army Military and Political School. The former faction consisted of bandits and thugs, while the latter consisted of young students, farmers, and workers. Guo concurrently served as the principal of the Red Army Military and Political School, where he formed a group to oppose Deng. When the plot was discovered, Guo and students Rao Bingkun, Lin Xiuhe, and Lin Kairong were arrested and executed by Deng. From then on, the struggle between the two factions intensified, leading to a sharp division. In October of last year, Deng Zihui led the pseudo-Twelfth Army and local Communists to attack Shanghang City. They engaged in fierce battles with the militia led by Wei Jiaren and were defeated by Luo, suffering heavy losses. Consequently, Deng accused Fu Bocui of ineffective combat and dismissed him from his military post, plotting to reorganize Fu's troops. In reality, Fu was a Trotskyist and was feared by Deng. After Fu was dismissed, Fu's troops remained scattered in Jiaoyang, loyal to Fu. Thus, the animosity between Fu and Deng grew. Deng, Zhang Dingchen, and others expelled Fu from the Communist Party. Shortly after, an assassination squad and a riot faction were discovered within the Red Army, aiming to eliminate cadre leaders and disrupt the Red Army's rule. Deng and others were greatly alarmed and determined that it was the work of the Trotskyist Social Democratic Party. On March 2nd, they launched a major purge, actively eliminating dissidents and establishing a Suppression of Counterrevolutionaries Committee. It is reported that Deng successively arrested over a thousand social democrats, imprisoning and killing them. Therefore, Fu vowed to be irreconcilable with Deng, engaging in several battles. As a result, Deng was severely defeated, retreating to Baitian, Dachi, and Xiaochi. This time, when Zhang Zhen's division arrived in Yongding to suppress the bandits, Fu did not assist Deng, leading to the Red Bandits' complete defeat and Zhang's division's subsequent recovery of Yongding. (April 7th)

Merger of Yucai Plants by Jin Province Government

▲Changing Military Industry Affiliates to Production Entities

Taiyuan Correspondence: The Yucai Steel Plant, Yucai Machinery Plant, and Military Horse Farm were previously transferred by the Jin-Sui Garrison Headquarters to the provincial government for management. The provincial government, considering that the Yucai Steel and Machinery Plants were fully equipped and of significant scale, but had only been used to supply materials to military factories, deemed it a waste. Therefore, adopting suggestions from various parties, it was decided to convert them into production entities. The 12th meeting yesterday resolved to merge the two plants, transform them into commercial enterprises, and manufacture machinery needed for production. It was named the Minsheng Steel and Machinery Plant. Starting from May 1st, the provincial government will subsidize the plant with 10,000 yuan per month. As for the former Military Horse Farm, due to poor management and the lack of necessity for continued existence, it was decided to abolish it, with its affairs merged into the Model Livestock Farm for management. The remaining horse breeds will reportedly be distributed to livestock farms in various regions for breeding with private horses to improve the breed. (April 8th)

Establishment of Harbin Municipal Party Headquarters

▲Holding the First Expanded Memorial Week

Harbin Correspondence: The Harbin Municipal Party Headquarters was officially established at 10:00 AM today (the 6th) at the Governor's Office and held its first expanded memorial week. Previously, after Wu Tiecheng arrived in Harbin, he repeatedly discussed the matter with the designated committee members Zhang Jinghui, Zhou Shouyi, and Xu Zhen on the 4th and 5th, deciding to establish the Party Headquarters before Zang Qifang and Zou Shangyou returned to Harbin. The internal organization would be discussed further when Zang and Zou returned. At 10:00 AM on the 6th, the Governor's Office auditorium was properly arranged and slogans were posted. Leaders from various agencies who attended included Li Shaogeng, Acting Director of the Chinese Eastern Railway; Shen Ruilin, Director; Zhao Jinlin, Chief of Staff of the Railway Protection Army Headquarters; Ding Chao, Garrison Commander of Binjiang; Xing Zhanqing, Brigade Commander of the 26th Brigade; Wang Ruihua, Chief of the Special Police Department; Song Wenyu, Mayor; Chen Kezheng, President of the Special District Court; Bao Lian, Director of the Department of Political Affairs, and dozens of others. Twenty years ago, many comrades, many martyrs, and many soldiers sacrificed everything to create the Republic of China as we know it today. After the ceremony, a group photo was taken, and the meeting adjourned. The gathering joyfully ended at 3:00 PM. It is reported that Mr. Wu is scheduled to depart for Heilongjiang tomorrow afternoon. (April 6th)

Anhui People Request the Formation of a Grain Management Committee

▲Advocating Centralized Wuhu and Restricted Exports

Wuhu Correspondence: Rice is a major product of Anhui Province, and the rice market firmly holds the overall commercial hub of the province, as well as being a major source of tax revenue. Since the implementation of 　Li, the Anhui Provincial Government, in order to make up for military and administrative expenses, had previously imposed a fee on rice exports. However, due to strong opposition from various parties, and the central government also upholding the original purpose of abolishing Li, an explicit order was issued to stop it, and it was cancelled at the end of last month. Recently, a Grain Management Bureau was re-established, and a strict ban on rice exports was imposed, which has caused disputes. Rice merchants and various industries have sent a flurry of letters and telegrams expressing their opposition. In addition to rice merchants appointing representatives Gu Houfu and Tao Yinhuai, together with chamber of commerce representatives Wu Xingju and Cui Lianggong, to petition the provincial government, Anhui people Xie Jingping and others have now submitted a petition to the provincial government, proposing the organization of a Grain Management Committee for the Central and Southern Routes of Anhui Province in Wuhu, in order to centralize registration, restrict exports, maintain food supplies, promote Wuhu's market, and preserve local education and charitable undertakings. The original petition is recorded as follows: "It is found that the output of the central and southern routes of Anhui Province is mainly rice, and the main export goods are also grain. Since the implementation of Li abolition, grain is tax-free, and the miscellaneous transportation of sailboats cannot be checked. Therefore, four harms have arisen. There has never been a restriction on grain exports from Anhui Province. Whenever there is a famine, there is a rice shortage. In the nineteenth year, foreign rice was purchased and subsidized at a price of twenty yuan per stone. Lessons from the past serve as a warning, and repeating the same mistakes is cause for concern. This is the first harm. Along the border of the Yangtze River, there are many ports and wharves. In the past, there were Li donation bureaus, which could be slightly checked. If there is no registration in the future, the people will have nothing to eat. Temporary restrictions will be ineffective. Smuggling and circumventing are impossible to prevent. Even if you want to ban it, what is the basis for it? This is the second harm. Wuhu is the only commercial port in Anhui Province, relying entirely on rice for economic circulation. With grain tax-free, all cities can export, without being limited to Wuhu. Trade in commercial ports has plummeted. This is the third harm. In the past, rice donations were heavily surcharged, and charities and education relied on them for subsidies. Now they are completely abolished, and most local undertakings have stagnated. This is a major concern for politics and culture. This is the fourth harm. Therefore, to maintain food supplies, exports must first be restricted. To restrict exports, registration must first be centralized. This is why the Grain Management Committee should be organized in Wuhu as soon as possible. What is meant by restricting exports? The number of grain exports from Hunan and Jiangxi is limited annually, depending on the abundance of the autumn harvest, but Anhui does not have this. It is urgent to emulate it. Moreover, in today's world, domestic investors have mostly moved to better locations because of bandit troubles. Therefore, households have little storage and warehouses have no grain reserves. When exporting, they only aim to make a profit, not hesitating to transport everything away. There is no preparation between the harvest seasons. If exports are not restricted, there will inevitably be a shortage every year. For the people, there is no greater disaster than this. What is meant by centralized registration? The borders of Anhui Province have many waterways, and leaks must be blocked for easy inspection. It is urgent to concentrate the rice from the central and southern routes in one port in Wuhu. Exports are not allowed elsewhere, and registration should be carried out as a basis for restriction. Moreover, the area within 200 li of Wuhu is a rice-producing area. News of high prices spreads quickly, and thousands of sails gather in the evening. Information is readily available, and transportation is convenient, unlike the roundabout and difficult transportation. The rice market has been established in Wuhu for decades, and the rice from central and southern Anhui has naturally gathered in Wuhu for a long time. There has been no harm to the sailing transport, and the current restrictions will not hinder it. The above two factors can achieve three benefits. Without centralization, it is impossible to check, how can registration be done? Without registration, there is no investigation, how can restrictions be done? Taking Wuhu as the rice export port for the central and southern routes, the government, together with the local authorities, forms the Grain Management Committee to investigate and register. Once a clear number is obtained, restrictions can be imposed at the discretion of the authorities, so that there will be no harm to farmers due to low prices or harm to merchants due to high prices. This is the benefit of maintaining food supplies. With the concentration of rice and the prosperity of trade, finance will circulate due to the accumulation of progress, and the trade of all goods will naturally flourish. Commercial affairs and all government affairs can be implemented, and construction undertakings can be achieved. This is the benefit of prospering commercial ports. With prosperous commerce and flourishing businesses, tax revenues will increase daily. All local charitable and educational undertakings will also gradually progress, not only preserving what already exists, but also making cultural and moral progress daily. This is the benefit of preserving local undertakings. Since the founding of the Republic of China, Wuhu's market has declined, and all industries have been abandoned. It is not too late to save it now. At this critical moment, the rice issue has arisen. It is reasonable to submit this petition for adoption and implementation."

Headquarters Announcement

The Desperate Situation of the Red Bandits in the Jiangxi Territory

Nanchang Correspondence: The Minister of Military Affairs, He Yingqin, has been in Jiangxi for nearly four months to supervise the suppression of the Red Bandits. In terms of military affairs, the 5th, 6th, 9th, 19th, and 26th Route Armies have extremely strong forces. At present, the scattered bandits in the rear have long been cleared. The general offensive against Zhu and Mao, who occupy Guangchang and Ruijin, began one day. The bandit-infested areas, such as Le'an, Yongfeng, Xingguo, and Yudu, have been successively recovered. Bandit dens such as Futian have also been destroyed one after another. Zhu and Mao's bandits are like fish in a kettle. Mr. He personally went to Ji'an by plane yesterday (the 9th) for an inspection. After returning to the province, in addition to issuing a statement, he also publicly announced the internal situation of the Red Bandits in Jiangxi and the progress of the National Army on all fronts, so that the general public would know the situation. The following is a record of the information obtained:

(1) The Strength and Occupied Locations of the Red Bandits in Jiangxi: 1. The 3rd Army, Huang Gonglue, has 7,000 to 8,000 men with over 5,000 guns. They are currently based in Yaotian, Shima, and Tengtian, and are the elite of the Red Bandits. They are divided into four regiments and are currently attempting to flee towards the border areas of Yudu and Xingguo. 2. The 4th Army, Lin Biao, has 6,000 men with over 4,000 guns. They are currently based in the Baishui Township area and are rumored to be fleeing towards Shicheng. 3. The 5th Army, Peng Dehuai, has 7,000 to 8,000 men with 6,000 guns. They are currently based in Shangzhuang, Pingtou, and Qingli, and are the elite of the Red Bandits. They are divided into five regiments and are currently attempting to flee towards the border areas of Xingguo and Yudu. 4. The 6th Army, Huang Zhidao, has 4,000 men with 1,300 to 1,400 guns. They are currently based in Donggu Mountain and Huocheng Gang and were newly formed from guns seized from the 18th Division. 5. The 7th Army, Li Wenlin, has 3,000 men with 1,200 to 1,300 guns. They are currently based in Futian and Donggu and are divided into three regiments. 6. The 8th Army, Xiang Ying, has 6,000 men with 5,000 to 6,000 guns. They are currently based in Liangcun, Longgang Xu, and Gulonggang Jiangkou and are the elite of the bandit army. Xiang Ying is the chairman of the Red Bandit Committee. It is rumored that this army is also under the command of Li Jie. 7. The 9th Army, Wu Zhonghao, has over 4,000 men with 1,200 to 1,300 guns. They are currently based in Futian and Chenggang. 8. The 10th Army, Yang Yuebin, has over 4,000 men with 1,300 to 1,400 guns. They are currently based in Longgang Tou. 9. The 11th Army, Gu Daozhong, has over 2,000 men with 700 to 800 guns. They are based between Ganzhu and Guangchang and are currently fleeing south. 10. The 12th Army, Luo Binghui, has 5,000 to 6,000 men with 3,000 guns. They are currently based in Donggu and Yangmei Ling, and a large part of them are currently fleeing towards Ruijin and Huichang. 11. The 20th Army, Liu Tiechao, has 1,400 to 1,500 men with over 1,000 guns. They are currently based in Shangshe and Gaoxing, and part of Zeng Bingchun's troops are scattered on the west bank of the Gan River, lurking between Suichuan and Yongxin. The 22nd Army, Chen Yi, has over 3,000 men with over 2,000 guns. They are currently based near Ruijin, and part of them are in the Chenggang and Futian areas. The Reserve 3rd Army, Zeng Zhengchu, has over 1,000 men with 400 to 500 guns. They are based between Shuinan and Shacun and are reorganized from the Red Guards, with no great ability. (The above bandits are all east of the Gan River, bordering western Fujian. Currently, their northeast, west, and south are all surrounded by the National Army, attacking them separately.) 12. The 7th Division of the 16th Army under Kong Hechong, Kong Hechong, has 5,000 to 6,000 men with 2,000 guns. The 8th Division, Zhang Tao, has over 2,000 men with 700 to 800 guns. The 9th Division, Li Youjun, has over 2,000 men with 700 to 800 guns. These bandits have fled from Huangmao, Cihua, and Zhutan to Lishi, which belongs to Pingxiang. Recently, they have fled from Lishi to Gaocun, which belongs to Wanzai County. Small groups are still scattered in Youju and Ma, which belong to Xiu, and Huishi and Tianbao, which belong to Yi. (The above bandits are currently being suppressed separately by the National Army's Tan Division in coordination with the 18th Division's Zhu Brigade and the Independent 32nd Brigade. Kong's bandits have been repeatedly defeated, and their strength has been greatly diminished.) 13. Liu Dexin's force has over 1,000 men with 600 to 700 guns, lurking in the mountains of Futian and Jintian. 14. Liu Wanchun's force has 700 to 800 men with 400 to 500 guns, lurking in the Yongxin Sanxi Xu area. 15. Zeng Bingchun's force has over 2,000 men with 800 to 900 guns, moving and looting in the various districts of Hexi, Suichuan, Taihe, Yongxin, and Ji'an. Recently, they have fled to Gaojia Xu and other places west of Anhe. 16. Li Mingrui's New 7th Army has over 1,000 men with 500 to 600 guns and is currently fleeing in Yongxin. Zhang Yi's unit has recently fled from Guidong in Hunan Province to Yongxin to join Li's unit. They were defeated west of Yongyang by our Luo Division, suffering heavy losses. (The above bandits are all west of the Gan River, looting and disturbing without a fixed location. They are currently being jointly suppressed by our Luo and Han Divisions in coordination with the Hunan Army, with considerable gains.) 17. The 10th Army, Zhou Jianping, has over 5,000 men with over 2,000 guns. They are currently fleeing in Guixi and Shangrao counties. They used to be based in Mount Mopan, but they have been repeatedly defeated in recent searches and suppressions by the National Army, suffering heavy losses. Their strength is now less than half. (The above is the bandit army in eastern Jiangxi. They are currently being searched and suppressed by the Ruan and Tang units and are nearing elimination.)

(2) The Cruel Situation of the Red Bandits: The methods used by the Red Bandits to massacre the people are too terrible to bear. In addition to beating, bayoneting, stabbing, and shooting, they would soak paper and cotton in kerosene, stick it to people's bodies, and set them on fire. They would also hang people upside down and pour boiling or cold water into their nostrils. In other counties, peasant bandits could arbitrarily arrest and kill people without the instructions of bandit leaders. Or even if they had paid to redeem themselves, they would still be arrested and killed. The bandit army has an organization called the "Suppression of Counterrevolutionaries Committee," whose meaning is to eliminate reactionary elements. The people they designate to be killed are Kuomintang members, AB Group members, local tyrants, landlords, capitalists, intellectuals, and National Army officers and soldiers. However, those whom the bandits call capitalists are even families with only four or five acres of land, who are regarded as small property owners and are all on the list to be killed. Those whom they regard as the intellectual class are slightly educated junior and senior primary school students, who are also on the list to be killed. As for the National Army soldiers, they initially use benefits and sex to lure them to surrender, but ultimately mistreat them and slaughter them all. Furthermore, according to actual investigations during the forty days of Ji'an's fall last year, 13,882 people were killed by the Red Bandits, and 20,798 people were abducted. The details are listed separately below:

County Number of People Killed Verified Unverified Number of People Abducted Verified Unverified

Ji'an 8,978 2,563 6,415 2,830 4,921 6,909

Yongxin 2,130 383 1,747 1,817 432 1,358

Secondly, in addition to arson, killing, robbery, and rape, the Red Bandits' barbaric and bestial acts against women are even more appalling. However, the bandits still glorify this as "liberation." In reality, it is no different from a demon seizing and devouring people. Wherever the Red Bandits arrive, any widow or virgin between the ages of 16 and 40 is arbitrarily taken to a certain team or association and forced into free and equal partnerships. If they slightly resist, they will be killed on the spot. Or if their husbands are not at home, or if they are considered the wives and daughters of reactionaries, they are forced to remarry freely. If they refuse, they will be killed. Their staff members, in groups, break into people's homes and boudoirs, arbitrarily tease and engage in beastly acts. If they resist slightly, they are given the name of reactionary and brutally killed.

(3) The Political Situation in Jiangxi Province: Since Jiangxi Province was devastated by the Red Bandits, the people have been displaced and the cities and villages have been reduced to ruins. Most of the farmers in the bandit areas have been forced into the Red Guards. Since the National Army has been working hard to search and suppress them, the bandit areas have been gradually reduced in size, and the people's hearts have gradually become stable. Recently, the county magistrates have been ordered to cooperate with the military to organize sentry teams in the recovered areas within a time limit, to strengthen the people's self-defense forces. At present, the most important political work is to recruit refugees and stabilize the people's hearts, to intensify anti-Red propaganda work, and to organize people's self-defense organizations. Other tasks, such as the selection of county governors, the implementation of disaster relief in the bandit areas, the adjustment of food supplies, the distribution of agricultural tools, and the opening up of transportation in the bandit areas, are all being actively carried out. A Jiangxi Local Reorganization Committee has also been established within the headquarters to plan the political facilities and all post-war affairs in the recovered areas, to stipulate procedures, and to supervise the implementation of them.

(4) Recent Progress in Suppressing Bandits and the Confiscation of Bandit Weapons: The large forces of the Red Bandits, such as Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang, are massed east of the Gan River, taking advantage of the rugged terrain in an attempt to resist stubbornly. Since the National Army began its separate suppression operations on the first of this month, significant progress has been made in just ten days. The bandits in places such as Shacun, Shangqi, Da Feng, Gu Bi, and Luo Jia Xu have been successively defeated by the National Army, with many captured. The National Army's front line has reached Longgang Tou, Jiangbei Dong, and the line east of Yudu, as well as Chenggang and Donggu Mountain. In the Nanfeng area, the National Army's progress has been even more rapid. Since the occupation of important places such as Liaobi, Baijin, Gan Shan, Qiacun, and Shuinan, its front line has approached the Ganzhu and Changqiao areas near Guangchang. Because the Red Bandits have been repeatedly defeated, they have fled in disarray towards Ningdu, Shicheng, and Ruijin. As for the western Jiangxi area, Tonggu and Yifeng have long been recovered by the National Army, and the bandits in the Jiugong Mountain and Xiaoyao Mountain areas have been successively eliminated. Kong Hechong's bandits have been repeatedly defeated by the National Army in Huanggang Kou, Huangmao, Cihua, and Jiangkou, and their strength has been greatly diminished. Li Mingrui's bandits recently joined forces with the pseudo-Independent Division of eastern Hunan, Tan Sicong, and the pseudo-20th Army, Zeng Bingchun, and other forces to attack Yongyang in an attempt to relieve the siege of Zhu and Mao. As a result, they were defeated again by the National Army's Luo unit, with over a thousand captured. The remnant bandits are still fleeing like rats towards the border of Hunan and will be extremely embarrassed. As for the bandit forces in eastern Jiangxi, such as Fang and Shao, they originally used the Mount Mopan area as their base. They have recently been searched and suppressed by the National Army on all sides and were defeated at Mingyang Pass, with over 400 bandits killed and countless weapons seized. The bandits' schools, repair shops, and pseudo-governments have all been burned down. As a result, the coerced peasant bandits have fled in droves, and their situation is desperate and nearing elimination. Since the National Army began its suppression operations, it has seized more than 3,000 bandit weapons. Recently, Zhu and Mao have disagreed again, and disputes have arisen from time to time. Not only is the infighting extremely fierce, but even public accusations have been made, and there is a strong sense of tension. Luo Binghui, who was originally a strong figure under Zhu's command, has long been jealous of Zhu. Recently, seeing Zhu's extraordinary tyranny, he broke away from Zhu and set up his own banner. Zhu resented him even more and thought about eliminating Luo every day. Therefore, Peng Dehuai and Huang Gonglue, seeing that Zhu Mao and others' ill feelings were deepening day by day and that a civil war was imminent, were eager to find their own way out and agreed to surrender to the National Army. This is because the Social Democratic Party in the Red Bandits is very active in the dark, carrying out its means of sowing discord. As a result, the number of those who opposed Zhu and Mao also increased daily. The National Army learned of this situation and took the opportunity to launch a fierce attack, winning victories and capturing many. And many people are carrying weapons to surrender. In this situation, the elimination of the Red Bandits is not far away.

Songjiang

Election of Executive Committee Members from Two Trade Associations: The South Goods, Tea, and Food Industry Association and the Hat Industry Association have completed preparations. A founding meeting was held at the Chamber of Commerce on the afternoon of the 13th. Ye Guanqun was dispatched by the County Party Headquarters to attend and provide guidance, and Qian Tiansheng, a clerk from the County Government, supervised the election. Chen Wenxiong presided over the Hat Industry Association, and Sun Shaochi presided over the South Goods, Tea, and Food Industry Association. Meetings were held successively, and the election results were as follows: Zhu Taisheng, Huang Ansheng, Yu Wanlan, Xia Zhensheng, Zhu Chunzhi, Chen Wenxiong, and Zhu Luquan were elected as executive committee members of the Hat Industry Association. For the South Goods, Tea, and Food Industry Association, Sun Shaochi, Fu Jinan, Zhang Yangqiao, Wang Jingqing, Cai Zhongyu, Ling Xiangshu, Fei Zuomei, Shen Shurong, and Jin Xianglin were elected as executive committee members. Sun Shaochi, Ling Xiangshu, and Jin Xianglin were recommended as standing committee members, with Sun Shaochi as the standing chairman.

Election Preparations for District Agricultural Education Association: The county's agricultural education organizations do not yet have a county-level organization, only five district education associations and four district agricultural associations have been established. Previously, the election supervisor ordered the supplementary creation of membership lists, but they have not been submitted. As a result, the voting records cannot be created. Therefore, a telegram was sent to each association to urgently create the lists overnight and submit them to the county government by the 16th of this month. In accordance with Article 7 of the Election Law, those qualified to represent the association should recommend one election supervisor and two voting and ballot counting administrators and submit their resumes to the county government for appointment. Furthermore, one person in charge must be designated to come to the county government at 2:00 PM on the 16th for a meeting regarding preparations for the election of representatives to the National Assembly. All relevant associations have been notified by telegram.

Kunshan

Robbery and Kidnapping by Bandits at Jiuli Bridge: On the evening of the 10th, the home of Fang Shiqing, a Shaoxing resident of Jiuli Bridge outside Xiaoximen, was invaded by six bandits who entered the inner room. Each held a handgun and forbade the family from making any noise. They robbed 400 silver dollars and, before leaving, kidnapped Shiqing's nephew, Deming. They also left a letter stating that five or six brothers had been dispatched to borrow 10,000 yuan in military funds, to be delivered to Room 1 of the Yadong Hotel on Wuma Road in Shanghai by the 27th day of the old calendar. Afterwards, the Fang family did not report the incident to the county for investigation. However, Wu Shaokang, the captain of the detective team, discovered the incident and reported it to the county government, which prepared a document and dispatched detectives and police officers to investigate.

Qingpu

Resolution of Labor-Capital Dispute in the Used Clothing Industry: In Zhujiege Town, Second District, workers in the used clothing industry have traditionally not received fixed salaries, only a commission of half a li. Recently, due to the increasing cost of living, all employees in the industry felt that 3.7 li per yuan was insufficient to maintain their livelihoods. On the 20th of last month, they sent representatives to negotiate with the employers several times, requesting an increase in commission. The employers showed no sincerity in responding. Later, they sent a letter to the trade association, requesting a general meeting to be convened and petitioning the County Party Headquarters to instruct the town's chamber of commerce to mediate with the employers. The town's chamber of commerce took responsibility for convening both parties for mediation, and the result was satisfactory. The original commission of half a li has been increased to 4.6 li per yuan.

Communist Suspects Transferred to Province for Trial: Yao and five others from Zhangliantang in the Third District of the county were arrested by the Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team on suspicion of being communists. They were transferred to the county government, and after repeated interrogations, no conclusive confession was obtained. Subsequently, an order was received from the province to transfer them to the province for trial. Yesterday, the prisoners were escorted to the province and transferred to the Special Military Court for trial.

Suzhou

Request to Establish a Relief Center for Unemployed Workers in the Wood Loom Industry: The Wuxian Silk Weaving Wood Loom Industry Association stated that Wuxian is a wealthy area with flourishing commerce. However, due to the impact of the current situation in recent years, all industries have declined, especially the yarn and satin industry, resulting in an increasing number of unemployed workers who are unable to survive. Therefore, they submitted a petition to the county government the day before yesterday, requesting that it be forwarded to the provincial government, requesting the establishment of a relief center for unemployed workers to provide relief.

Large Group of Lake Bandits Arrives at Maoqi Port Again: Yesterday morning, a large group of lake bandits from Zhejiang Province arrived near Maoqi Port in Taihu Lake. The bandits, numbering over a hundred, boarded more than twenty ships and planned to rob fishing boats in the area. The resident water and land police team received a report and rushed to suppress them. The bandits fled back to Zhejiang Province.

Wuxi

Daytime Robbery by Deserter: Zhu Chen, a resident of Nanshi Bridge Xia Tang in the city (wife of Zhu Shigui, former Chief of the Works Section of the Municipal Preparatory Office), was returning home from shopping in Beimen around 6:00 PM the day before yesterday. While passing under the Zhongshi Bridge, she was suddenly stopped by a deserter wearing a worn-out uniform. The deserter snatched the wallet (said to contain a 100-yuan postal money order and four silver dollars) from Zhu Chen's hand and fled. Zhu Chen immediately shouted for help. The police officer on duty nearby heard the cry and came forward, capturing the deserter. The deserter was taken to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau. According to his confession, his name was Li Weide, 22 years old, from Sichuan. He was a soldier under his commander but was discharged. Because he had no money to return home, he resorted to this desperate measure. Director Gao, based on the confession, prepared a document and transferred him to the General Bureau for interrogation.

Summary of Resolutions from the County Party Consolidation Conference: The County Party Consolidation Conference held its 104th Committee Meeting yesterday. The resolutions of important cases are summarized as follows: (1) The Provincial Party Consolidation Conference issued an order requiring comrades in the province to donate to the Central Construction Fund, to be completed before the end of May. Resolved: Comply with the order. (2) Feng Xitang and others, organizers of the County Farmers' Association, reported that they had no funds for April and requested assistance to complete their work. Resolved: Recommend committee members to contact the County Government for assistance. (3) The former Pawnshop Workers' Union reported that the employers disregarded laws and regulations and did not provide holidays on national commemorative days, requesting correction in accordance with the law to maintain Party discipline. Resolved: Hand over to the training officer for review. (6) A report stated that Qian Zhaoyi, a citizen of the First District (i.e., Qian Zhongliang, head of the First District), had illegally constructed a building, which seriously hindered municipal administration. How should the association respond? Resolved: Investigate and handle the matter jointly with the Construction Bureau.

Murder Case: Another Suspect Apprehended: Guo Zizhen, a villager from Dai Lane, Furong Mountain, in the Sixth District (Tianxia Market), was brutally beaten to death by villagers from three neighboring lanes on March 24th of the 17th year of the Republic. Afterwards, the victim's family reported the case, and several people were arrested and detained. It is now learned that Guo's wife, Mao, reported to the 12th Branch of the Public Security Bureau the day before yesterday, stating that Ni He, Ni Renquan, and Li Agou, all involved in the case, were playing in Doushan and requested the police to arrest them immediately. Upon receiving the report, Branch Chief Tan immediately dispatched police to arrest Li Agou, but the others escaped. He was immediately taken to the bureau and interrogated. After a preliminary trial, a document was prepared and transferred to the Public Security Bureau for further investigation.

Soliciting Opinions on Final Accounting Period: The Shanghai Money Industry Association previously stated that determining the national industrial and commercial accounting year based on the Shanghai Social Bureau's proposal to set the end of February as the final accounting period had various obstacles. It advocated setting the end of January as the final accounting period for appropriateness. It detailed the reasons in a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce for adoption and also sent a circular to the Money Industry Associations of various counties for support to achieve consistency. The Wuxi Money Industry Association approved the letter, believing that this matter was of great importance to commerce. It immediately convened all members to discuss and unanimously agreed with Shanghai's proposal. It resolved to set the period from January 21st to January 30th each year as the preparation period for closing, January 31st as the final accounting period, and February 1st to February 20th as the investigation and consolidation period. It also resolved to send a letter to the Shanghai Money Industry Association for reconsideration and a letter to the Zhenjiang Money Industry Association to convene a joint meeting of the Jiangsu Provincial Money Industry Association for in-depth discussion to ensure that the opinions of various regions and industries were consistent. At the same time, it also sent letters to chambers of commerce and other industries soliciting opinions.

Consolidating Township Shop Tax: After the Financial Bureau took over the direct collection of shop taxes in the townships, it dispatched Pan Gongpu and others to conduct a thorough survey in the townships. The survey has been completed, and the monthly collection is estimated to be around 860 yuan, with an annual collection of over 10,320 yuan, more than double the original collection. The report has been submitted to the County Government for approval.

Special Products Association Sends Personnel to Collect Products: The Ministry of Industry's National Products Exhibition Hall's Provincial Special Products Exhibition will begin with Jiangsu Province this year and is scheduled to open on May 5th and last for one month. The Wu County Chamber of Commerce received an official letter from the hall yesterday (13th), requesting assistance in collecting products for display and dispatching Qiu Jun, a staff member of the hall, to Changzhou to handle the collection of products and investigate special products. Sea and Land Boy Scouts Walk to Changzhou: The Jinghu Line Long-Distance Walking Tour Group of the Sea and Land Boy Scouts Training Class of the Shanghai China Sports School, consisting of 19 male and female members led by Chief Instructor Chen Meiqing, walked to Changzhou from Wuxi on the 12th. They planned to visit Tianning Temple, Wenbi Pagoda, Xuanmiao Temple, and parks on the morning of the 13th.
