Jinshan

Notorious Bandit Yao Xingsheng Captured: Yao Xingsheng, a notorious bandit, is a resident of Qianjiawei, East of the Twenty-fifth Tu. Since joining Taibao Ashu's gang last year, he has specialized in kidnapping for ransom, arson, and robbery. The local people who have suffered from his poison cannot be enumerated. This spring, military police conducted repeated searches and suppressions, but he remained at large. Yesterday (12th), Xingsheng suddenly sneaked back home. The water patrol team stationed in Kongjiaque learned of this and was led by Deputy Captain Ge and Patrol Officer Shen Zugen to surround and capture him. When the bandit saw the military police coming to arrest him, he attempted to escape by wading through the water. However, Deputy Captain Ge shot and injured him, and he was captured. The bandit initially denied it, but after being identified by acquaintances, he admitted without hesitation. A Mauser rifle and 26 rounds of ammunition were also found in his home. He was immediately taken to the team for interrogation.

Jiashan

Change of Commander in Water Police Team: Xiong Mengzhao, commander of the Seventh Team of the Second District of the Water Police stationed in Ganyao, received an order from the province to be transferred to the province for reassignment. The vacancy was filled by Dong Yashu. It is feared that Commander Dong has already arrived in Gan on the 11th to take over.

Reorganization and Establishment of County Farmers' Association: The County Farmers' Association was ordered to reorganize the day before yesterday. Gu Fenglai, Gu Youzheng, Yong Sheng, Xie Pinrong, Shen Shipei, Huang Xuezhi, and Chen Jianpei were elected as directors, with Gu Jinlan and Wang Changfa as alternates. Gu Fenglai was elected as Director-General, Chen Jianpei as Deputy Director-General, and Hong Boming as Secretary. Today, they took over all documents managed by the former County Farmers' Association and began work.

Nantong

Formation of Coastal Fishing Protection Team: The Jiangsu Coastal Fishing Protection Office was jointly established by the Provincial Government Pacification Superintendent's Office, the Naval Department, and the National Coastal Patrol Department. The National Army Provincial Security Regiment stationed in Tong and the marines from ships such as Tongji were reorganized into the Coastal Fishing Protection Team. Zhang Han, the Wusong Water Police District Chief, led police ships to Tong on the 12th to join the bandit suppression. A small criminal short-wave radio station was set up on the second floor of the Nantong Club to transmit military information. Regarding the allocation of Zhang Shen's rebellious property, organizations such as the Tongyi Baotang Association presented petitions to the Provincial Government, requesting that funds be allocated from Zhang Shen's rebellious property confiscated by the county for subsidies. On the 12th, the Provincial Government ordered the County Government to investigate the confiscated rebellious property and use it specifically for education and relief in accordance with the regulations. Whether the requested allocation for Baotang and other expenses can be approved will be determined by the Civil Affairs Department after verification.

Zhenjiang

Counties Rush to Collect Agricultural Education Registers: The Jiangsu Provincial Office for the Election of National Assembly Representatives prepared the general register of electors, ballot papers, and ballot boxes for agricultural education organizations. It telegraphed election supervisors in various counties to select suitable personnel to come to the provincial office before the 13th to collect them for use in their counties. Suqian, Guanyun, Jintan, Dongtai, Changshu, Yixing, Qidong, Chongming, Funing, Shuyang, Gangshan, Xinghua, Huai'an, Guancheng, Siyang, Lianshui, Huaiyin, Gan, Pizhou, and over twenty other counties sent people to collect them. The office was extremely busy issuing ballot boxes. The receiving and dispatching section was also swamped with reports from various counties on the results of elections in industrial and commercial organizations, due to the approaching deadline. The reports were sent by mail or special delivery. It is heard that the announcement and election dates for the second phase of organizations will be slightly different from those of the first phase of industrial and commercial organizations. The announcement period is from April 17th to 19th, and the election voting period is April 20th and 21st. In addition to telegraphing the election supervisors in various counties to comply, those sent to collect the election registers must be informed and instructed to pass on the information to avoid delays.

Reappointment of Fifth Branch Chief: Ma Yuebo, the former chief of the Fifth Branch of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, was dismissed for soliciting excessive fees. Qiu Yongtu, a bureau staff member, was appointed as acting chief. The matter was immediately reported to the Civil Affairs Department. Yesterday, the Public Security Bureau was notified that the dismissal of Ma's position was approved and that Pan Rugang was appointed as the new chief of the Fifth Branch. Pan took office after receiving the order.

Yangzhong

Election of Party Member Representatives to National Assembly: Yangzhong County held the election of Party member representatives to the National Assembly on the 10th, with voting held in the district branches in the morning and afternoon. The County Party Headquarters and the County Election Supervisor dispatched personnel to supervise the elections in various rural areas. The total vote count was completed on the same day, and Niu Yongjian, Ye Xiufeng, Huang Yuren, Yang Xingqin, and Wang Kaoying received the most votes. Zhu Wenzhong, Pan Guojun, Di Ying, and others also received several votes. The results have been telegraphed to the province for reporting.

Robbery and Kidnapping at Gongxin Bridge: A Sun family in Gongxin Bridge, Yangzhong County, who were of moderate wealth, were suddenly attacked by over forty bandits from Jiangbei on the evening of the 6th. Silver and jewelry worth over 1,000 yuan were robbed. Before leaving, the bandits kidnapped the head of the household, Mr. Sun, and his whereabouts are unknown.

Fire in Xinglong Town: Xinglong Town in the county is a small market town. The night before last, a fire broke out in a thatched shed and spread to over ten shops and houses, including those of Gu Changshou, Zhu Yuanqing, Shi Gaogui, Zhong Yancai, Gao Shugui, Tu Deyang, and Tu Wang. The losses are estimated to be over 3,000 yuan.

Gaoyou

Kidnapping and Robbery in the Third District: The home of Xu Yongbiao, a farmer in Xiachun Village, Bazong, Third District of the county, was suddenly attacked by seven bandits armed with guns the night before last. They kicked open the door and robbed everything. Before leaving, they kidnapped his five-year-old son, claiming that someone should be sent to Bali Song within ten days to contact someone holding a red lantern. Later, they went to the nearby Nanjiaodun and kicked open the door of farmer Feng Baotang's house, conducting a thorough search. Over 160 silver dollars and clothing were robbed. Before leaving, they also kidnapped his three-year-old son, instructing his family to prepare 3,500 yuan and go to Bali Song within ten days to redeem him.

Jiaxing

Change of Warden at Branch Court Detention Center: Jin Pinshan, the warden of the Jiaxing Branch Court Detention Center, was ordered to be transferred to Hangzhou County Local Court as a detention official. He took office in Hangzhou the day before yesterday. The position of warden of the Jiaxing Branch Court Detention Center has been filled by Wang Cheng, appointed by the High Court. Wang came to He on the 13th to take office after receiving the appointment.

Bengbu

Bandit Involved in Robbery of Steamer Executed by Firing Squad: After the Tongji steamer sailing from Bengbu to Zhengyang last month was robbed between Shitouping and Jia Tan, Ni Rongxian, the temporary bandit suppression commander of Shoufeng Huai counties, and the chief of the First District of the Changhuai Water Public Security Bureau arrested several bandits involved in the robbery, including Wang Chaoxue, Xun Guohao, and Liao Duofu. They were transferred to Bengbu and submitted to the Anhui Northern Garrison Headquarters for handling. After the military court of the headquarters interrogated them, Liao Duofu and the other two bandits confessed to the crime of robbery and kidnapping. Wei Linghuang, the commander of the headquarters, approved the death sentence. At around 9:00 AM on the 11th, the Garrison Headquarters presented the case of the three criminals, verified their identities, and sent a team to the Heng Railroad execution ground on Erma Road to carry out the execution by firing squad.

Banditry in Northern Anhui's Suxian County: Suxian County in northern Anhui borders Jiangsu and Henan and has the most bandits of any county. Sanbahou, a notorious bandit, previously gathered four to five hundred people near Jiagu and occupied the area for robbery and harassment. After repeated suppressions by the local militia, they mostly fled to Xishan. Recently, there has been no banditry. However, the bandit forces in the northwest of the county have become rampant again. The bandit leaders Zhang Chuanwen, Yu Keming, Zhou Laohai, and others recently led over a hundred fierce bandits to attack Tanshanwei. The stockade is located in the mountains and is a transportation hub between Suixi and Caili. The terrain is dangerous. The bandits attacked from the east, west, and south sides, very fiercely. The defenders on the east side saw the bandits' fierceness and were unable to resist, and there was a tendency to abandon the defense. Seven or eight fierce bandits took the opportunity to scale the wall and attack with guns. In a critical situation, the stockade leader Zhang Daolong ordered the stockade houses to be closely guarded and led people to fight the bandits in the streets. The bandits in the stockade were killed. At the same time, the nearby militia arrived after hearing the alarm and attacked from inside and outside. The bandits were defeated and fled, leaving over ten bandits dead and over ten bandits wounded. Over ten bandit guns were captured, and the bandit leader Zhou Laohai was killed on the spot.

Letters

Letter from Lvcheng Elementary School, Danyang County

To the editor of your esteemed newspaper:

Upon reviewing your newspaper's local correspondence column on April 7th, the article "Tragedy at School Sports Meet in Our County" stated that a student from our school was hit in the face by a shot put. This is inconsistent with the facts. The student was accidentally hit on the head by a shot put while he was practicing, but he did not suffer any serious injuries. He walked as usual at the time. The report that his facial bones were shattered and that his life was in danger is a fabrication by the contributor to mislead the public. We hereby send a letter of correction, hoping that it will be published in the "Letters" column to clarify the truth and conform to the facts. Lvcheng Elementary School, Danyang County, March 11th.

Letter from Judge Gu Yushang, Changshu County

To the editors of Shanghai Shen Bao:

I have read your newspaper's Changshu correspondence column on April 12th, which stated that the High Court transferred Judge Gu Yushang of Changshu to be a clerk at the Shanghai District Court because he was unclear about the case. The vacancy was filled by a prosecutor from Wujin Court acting as an agent. I have not violated any laws in judging cases, and the High Court has not made any transfer news. It is very surprising where your newspaper obtained this news. This matter is detrimental to my reputation, so I am sending a telegram to clarify and request a correction.

Educational News

Special Article

Life at Wellesley College (II)

By Miss Lu Er Zhao, sent from the United States

(3) In this school, all staff members, from the president down, never look down on the working students. The black female workers employed by the school go home after lunch on Sundays. (The female employees of the school do not live at the school, they come in the morning and leave in the evening, like commuting students. In the morning, they greet each other with "Good morning," and in the evening, they say "Goodbye.") Therefore, on Sunday evenings, Er Zhao and Miss Xie work together to cook and bake bread to fill their stomachs. The cleaning and tidying of the bedrooms are done by the students themselves, every day, and this becomes a habit. The daughter of a wealthy capitalist also operates in the same way at the school, as a matter of course. So, the departure of the female workers has nothing to do with us. Every year, tens of thousands of American university graduates find it difficult to find a suitable position. When necessary, male graduates mostly work temporarily as clerks, such as waiters in restaurants and assistants in grocery stores. Female graduates mostly work as secretaries, accountants, and hairdressers. So, when we see young men and women in restaurants and stores serving attentively and behaving generously, we always pay more attention to them. The most valuable and unbreakable thing in the world is the element of self-reliance. During the student years, during the holidays or after school hours, one should seek a social position to practice one's abilities. Books are dead, and affairs are alive. Reading is for application and for doing things. If one only reads dead books, then one is just a book basket or a bookworm and not very helpful to society. To seek application, one must first seek employment. Employment must be regarded as equal, and one must strive for progress. In American families, housewives and their children mostly do their own cleaning, tidying, cooking, and clothing. First, labor costs are expensive and not easy to hire. Second, doing chores oneself can save money on materials. Children can also prepare for the world in the future. It is a good thing to have several benefits at once.

(4) American girls are very lively and have developed a habit of loving sports since childhood. Special rewards are given to those who enter university. The method is that only those whose scores in each subject are above 70 points (Grade C) are selected as players. Otherwise, they are rejected. Those who are not selected suffer great humiliation. Loving fame is a common trait of human beings. What is the pain in the hearts of those who love sports but are refused? For example, a child who loves snacks has snacks in front of him but cannot eat them. Others are eating them in front of him with relish, and this greedy child can see them but cannot eat them. What is his pain? Westerners call it the torture of the stomach. American girls whose scores are not full of 70 points are no different from being led. How can each subject not be diligently pursued? Also, the height of American girls is generally longer than that of our Chinese girls, but there is still not much difference. However, the hands and feet are very different. There is always a special feeling when shaking hands or holding hands. After swimming, when wearing shoes, one sees that the shoes of classmates in the same team are arranged in one place. In comparison, most are about one-half inch longer. It can be seen that women in that country use more strength and have longer thigh muscles. Physiological relations and habits are natural and cannot be achieved overnight. Our classmates here have never fallen behind in their scores in various subjects, but they always cannot take the lead in physical education. This is the cause of inner guilt, and they are working hard to strive.

The above four aspects are just a rough outline. Perhaps some say that American women have many strengths and no shortcomings? Er Zhao must answer that they are inevitable, but we are here to study, determined to take their strengths to make up for our weaknesses. We cannot but use a realistic approach to describe the general situation of our life at this school for the past six months. It is not our intention to be pretentious or to create something new. Yesterday at noon, it was raining and snowing, and the campus was all white. (December 19th at noon, which is about 10:00 PM on the 18th of the same month in our country.) Georgia, in the southern United States, rarely snows. Now, fortunately, seeing it, the students were all carrying their schoolbags, rejoicing and going crazy. They were trampling on snow, holding snow, dancing snow, throwing snow, and making snowballs, each enjoying their freedom. Er Zhao and Miss Wu also played in the snow for a while. In the evening, snow mist, the snow outside the window has not melted, so I wrote a rhyme to leave a footprint.

Remotely separated from my parents by 30,000 miles, studying alone in the Western Hemisphere, the rivers and mountains are all bright brocade, today the rain and snow do not fall in the Jiang Village,

Last year, my father also wrote poetry, my younger brother and I stepped on the snow, today, Georgia comes to appreciate the snow, I know my mother is longingly thinking. (The End)

Important News

Sino-French Expedition

丨French Side's Independent Action丨

▲Chu Minyi Sternly Negotiates

丨If No Result, Cooperative Agreement Will Be Cancelled丨

▲Crawling Vehicles Proceed from Changping, North of Kou, to Zhanghuan

▲Vehicles Only Fly French Flags, No Chinese Flags

Report from Beiping on the 10th: After the Sino-French Academic Expedition's crawling vehicles fell into the water at Shahe, they were originally scheduled to depart north the day before yesterday. However, because they were waiting for the French driver to arrive, they stopped there. Mr. Chu Minyi led team members to the site yesterday morning to inspect. The vehicles were still parked in the old city of Changping County. The Ford car that fell into the water and was damaged the day before yesterday was reportedly hired from Tianjin and has been repaired. It was driven back to Tianjin yesterday. The seven crawling vehicles are all intact and are scheduled to continue driving to Nankou yesterday afternoon. If there are no delays, they should reach Nankou last night. However, each vehicle flies a French flag at the front, and no Chinese flag is visible. It is said that academic circles are extremely indignant upon seeing this. After inspecting the site, Chu Minyi returned to Beiping at 6 PM yesterday. He is scheduled to negotiate with the French side tonight with Xu Bingchang and Ma Heng based on the original cooperative method and the principles discussed at the Antiquities Association the day before yesterday. If there is no result, the cooperative agreement between the two parties will be cancelled. However, because these vehicles are bulky, once they have set off, it is quite difficult to turn them back. Therefore, the Chinese side only requires the French side to abide by the Chinese side's restrictions and legal inspection procedures in the future. The Chinese team members will take the Ping-Sui train from Beiping to Zhanghuan and depart on schedule, it is said.

▲Original Text of the Cooperative Method

The Chinese Academic Societies Association, in order to organize an academic expedition and cooperate with Mr. Arthaud of France within Chinese territory, has established the following cooperative method: Article 1: This Association, in order to develop academic studies and accommodate Mr. Arthaud's assistance, has formed the Academic Expedition. Article 2: This Association, based on this cooperative method, will supervise and direct all matters related to the expedition's activities. Article 3: The Academic Expedition will be organized by a number of Chinese and French team members appointed by this Association. The French team members among them will be appointed after being reviewed by this Association. Their names, qualifications, and subjects they are responsible for will be listed separately in an attachment. Article 4: This Association will appoint one Chinese and one French head from among the team members. Article 5: The duties of the Chinese and French heads are defined as follows: (1) The Association will generally define the conduct and working hours during the journey, etc. However, if there is a need for changes due to factual circumstances, the Chinese and French heads may negotiate and change them. (2) The Chinese and French heads will negotiate and determine the distribution of work among the team members. (3) The Chinese head will preside over matters relating to communication with local officials along the way. (4) The Chinese head will preside over the transportation of collected items. Article 6: The allocation of national expenses and other necessary matters during the journey are stipulated as follows: (1) All travel expenses for Chinese team members from Beijing to Tacheng or Yili, and from Annam back to Beiping, will be entirely borne by this Association. (2) All food, tents, porters, vehicles, medicine, and transportation costs for collected items, as well as other necessary expenses for the entire team from the date of departure from Tacheng or Yili to the date of arrival in Annam after the completion of the expedition, will be borne by the French side. (3) Any other matters not covered will be handled by the Chinese head in consultation with the French head at any time and reported to this Association for assessment. Article 7 (Route to be determined). Article 8: The duration of the journey shall not exceed one year. Article 9: The main subjects of investigation during the journey are geography, geology, biology, anthropology, archaeology, and folklore. Article 10: This Association requests the General Staff Headquarters to send a special commissioner to join the team. All matters directly or indirectly related to China's national interests or national rights must not be investigated. If there are any violations, the special commissioner of the General Staff Headquarters shall stop them at any time. Article 11: Foreigners are not allowed to survey and map during the journey. Article 12: The following regulations should be observed during the investigation: (1) No historical or artistic buildings shall be damaged under any pretext. (2) No antiques shall be purchased in a private capacity, etc. Article 13: The archaeological regulations do not allow excavation work. However, small-scale excavations will not have a major impact on the country's progress. In addition, items obtained from excavation that are not too heavy and do not require special equipment for transportation may be carried out by the Chinese head in consultation with the French head. Article 14: The method of disposing of items collected or excavated is stipulated as follows: (1) Archaeological items must be handed over to the Chinese head or the Chinese team members entrusted by them for transportation back to this Association for preservation. (2) For geological or biological items, the method is the same as above. However, after being transported back to Beiping, a copy will be given to the French side after review by this Association. Article 15: The method of disposing of the various achievements obtained from the investigation is stipulated as follows: (1) Photos must be submitted to this Association for review, and one copy must be deposited with this Association. (2) Scientific diagrams and records must be submitted to this Association for review and completed within six months. (3) Notes, drawings, or diaries shall be handled in accordance with the above articles. (4) Films: (1) When taking films, the Chinese head must appoint Chinese team members to monitor them at all times and send the films back to Beiping for review by this Association. (2) Two copies must be deposited with this Association.

"Attachment 1" However, team members are also allowed to purchase small antiques. If there is any doubt, it must still be reviewed by the Chinese Academic Societies Association. (Note: The Sino-French Scientific Expedition was initially named the Academic Expedition).

Various Counties

Popular Public Lecture Halls

丨To Improve Public Education丨

▲The Two Ministries of Interior and Education Consulted on Measures to Submit to the Executive Yuan for Approval. The Complete County Organization Law was originally scheduled to be completed uniformly by the 19th year of the Republic [1930], but because various provinces were unable to complete it as scheduled, it has now been extended to the end of this year. County autonomy will be completed by the end of the 23rd year of the Republic [1934]. All procedures will still be handled as before. It is heard that the two Ministries of Interior and Education, in view of the fact that the period of autonomy is being handled, believe that popularizing public education is extremely important. They have specially consulted on holding public lecture halls and ordered the various district offices to handle them, in order to provide the public with opportunities to become literate and facilitate autonomy. All measures have been consulted on and submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval.

Middle School Student Party Principles Essay Awarded Yesterday

Yesterday, the Training Department of the Municipal Party Headquarters held the Shanghai Municipal Student Party Principles Essay Award Ceremony during the Memorial Week. A total of eight outstanding students from the high school and junior high school groups attended (Wang Yunbai, Qian Yeqiu, and Qiu Xiseng from Wuben were absent). Around 11 o'clock, the Memorial Week was about to end, and Tong Hangbai, the Minister of the Municipal Training Department, reported: (1) The purpose of holding the competition is to encourage middle school students' interest in the study of Party Principles and to train their ability to sell and develop well. (2) The processing lasted for four months, half of which was spent waiting for submissions and half for careful review. (3) As a result, each of the two groups had five selected and five alternates to prevent any undiscovered talents. The students received the awards in turn, and their faces were filled with joy, regarding it as the highest honor. New News from the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center

Mr. Pan Yangyao, Deputy Director of the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center, went to Liaoning on the 19th of last month to inspect the developed vocational education in Liaoning. He received a warm reception from the local education community and was invited by Mr. Pan to plan to improve Shenyang Nongfu and contact to organize a vocational guidance center, which was extremely busy. Mr. Pan and others transferred to Japan on the 6th of this month to inspect vocational education. They believe it is very developed, especially supplementary education, which is set up for young people who are going to school and employment. There are 43 vocational introduction offices in Tokyo, divided into general, labor, intellectual class, women, and juvenile categories. The Central Vocational Introduction Office is the largest. Mr. Pan is visiting every day and will soon have a detailed report to contribute to the country. It is also reported that the Japanese Chinese Youth Association also has a proposal to organize a vocational guidance center, and the realization of the period is not far away. Recently, the Institute was entrusted by a large machine factory in Shenyang to find factory management talents, with graduates from domestic and foreign universities of engineering with factory management experience as qualified. A large silk weaving factory in this city has entrusted the recruitment of a salesperson, with mechanical knowledge and commercial experience and familiarity with the factory situation as qualified. In addition, a large well-known factory in this city has entrusted the invitation of several calligraphy talents, with the ability to write various fonts such as Zheng Li Wei, or art fonts and art English letters as qualified. Soccer Friendly

Fu Jen and Jinan Face Off

▲4:00 PM Today at the Baseball Field

Chinese Baseball Association Established

▲Practice Begins This Wednesday

Baseball in Shanghai has always been underdeveloped. However, in previous years, the Chinese baseball team still had a considerable reputation and twice represented East China to win the National Regional Baseball Championship. Unfortunately, the person in charge was not his person last year, which led to the invisible disappearance. At present, the veterans on the sea have decided to retrain the new army and organize a team to promote it. A meeting was specially convened at the YMCA Sports Department at 5:30 yesterday afternoon. Because of the previous disorganization, it was decided to formally establish the Chinese Baseball Association. The staff will be elected at the next plenary meeting. If Westerners in Shanghai initiate a joint competition, they will send a team to participate. It is not to win, but to learn from each other's baseball skills and add a different color to Shanghai's naive Chinese baseball community. The first practice is scheduled for this Wednesday, the second is scheduled for Saturday, and three times a week thereafter. Those who attended the meeting yesterday included Lin Wencheng, Lin Wenfa, Wu Zhichao, Lun Jinchang, Chen Zhongle, Huang Zhonghui, Zhou Chongdao, Zeng Guangbang, Feng Chaoliang, Wu Zhenbang, Gu Degang, Li Baojun, Zhang Guoxun, Ren Jiexing, Ye Guihong, Pang Qingfang, Liu Dacheng, etc. All those with considerable skills in baseball are expected to join.

丨Held at 10:00 AM丨

▲City Trams and Buses All Stopped

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau will hold a long-distance race next month on the 19th at 10:00 AM next to the Chen Yingshi Martyrs Memorial Tower in the West Gate. On the same day, the trams and buses on the way should be temporarily stopped when the racers pass by, etc. This order is hereby issued to the company to comply with and handle it."

Beijing-Ping Line

Flights Will Begin Tomorrow Morning

▲The Tianjin Station Will Not Stop Temporarily

The Beijing-Ping line, which has been planned for a long time by China Airlines, has decided to start Beijing-Ping flights tomorrow morning (the 15th). The arrangement of the airport along the station and the installation of radio equipment have only not been completed at the Tianjin station. The rest are ready, so the Beijing-Ping flight will not stop at the Tianjin station tomorrow morning. The northbound plane will take off from Beijing at 8:30 and arrive in Xu at 10:30. It will arrive in Jinan at 12:30. The plane will fly directly to Beijing when it reaches Jinan Station, and arrive in Ping at 3:20 in the afternoon. The southbound plane will take off from Ping at 8:00, arrive in Jinan at 10:40, arrive in Xu at 12:40, and arrive in Beijing at 2:50. The entire route is 1,200 kilometers long and takes only seven hours to pass through the stations. The plane will stop for ten minutes at each station to load and unload mail. The Pingjin currently in Ping is needed for the southbound flight tomorrow morning. The pilot is assigned to Hao Zhonghe to drive. The Beijing-Jinan No. 2 is located at the Ming Palace Airport in Beijing. Zhang Huaiyi has been assigned as the pilot for the northbound flight tomorrow morning. The Xu and Bengbu aircraft were originally needed for the Beijing-Ping aircraft to fly against each other. They are currently being repaired in Shanghai and will soon be transported to the Beijing station for use. It is found that the aircraft on the Beijing-Ping line are all Steinson land aircraft with a load of 800 pounds (each pound is 450 grams). The flights within the two-month period will only carry mail and will not carry passengers. Passengers will be carried two months later. The aircraft carrying mail will also change and increase or decrease with the aircraft load. Nie Kaiyi is currently handling various matters in Tianjin. Yesterday afternoon, Mr. Nie sent a telegram to Shanghai saying that he would take a plane south to Ping tomorrow morning, stay in Beijing that day, and go to the Ministry of Communications the next day to report and contact various matters in Tianjin.

Guangdong

Aviation Status and Aviation Conference

▲ Mr. Liu Zhiyan's Remarks

Mr. Liu Zhiyan, representative of the Guangdong Aviation Authority to the National Aviation Conference (currently the acting principal of the Guangdong Aviation School), arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong on the 12th and stayed at the Dongya Hotel. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency inquired about the recent situation of Guangdong aviation and his mission to attend the National Aviation Conference in Beijing. Mr. Liu replied that the Guangdong Aviation Department originally had the First and Second Air Squadrons. On the first of this month, a new Third Squadron was established. Given Guangdong's limited territory, having three air squadrons, supplemented by several Curtis Hawk fighter planes, the strength is not weak. In terms of civil aviation, the Guangzhou to Wuzhou route is already in operation. The Guangdong to Zhongshan County and Guangzhou to Shantou routes will also be launched soon. Regarding the school, the most recent graduating class (the fourth class) has been assigned to various squadrons. Additionally, eight individuals have been ordered by the Aviation Department Director to work in Hunan. These individuals will first go to Beijing for instructions. Currently, the school has one class of the fifth class and is continuing to recruit sixty students for the sixth class, who can enroll soon. This is a general overview of the recent situation of Guangdong aviation. As for my being dispatched to Beijing this time to attend the National Aviation Conference, I am accompanying Director Huang (Guangrui) to Shanghai. We will stay for a few days and then go to Beijing. I also plan to propose twelve motions, such as formulating aviation laws and regulations, establishing a national aviation meteorological system, night flight facilities, establishing a central aviation university, and mapping aviation maps. These are all crucial plans. However, convening the conference has even greater significance. If a second world war occurs, China will definitely be drawn into the whirlpool. There is no possibility of neutrality. The French General Foch even said that future world wars will be won by the air force. The status of the air force today is not what it used to be. How can we strengthen the air force? If we are drawn into a world war, we can also deal with foreign countries. We must plan ahead and be prepared. I am very optimistic about this conference, etc. It is noted that Mr. Liu graduated from the Aviation University in the United States and then from the Aviation University in Russia. His experience and knowledge are excellent.

Taxpayers' Association to Hold Executive Committee Meeting Today

▲ Mutual Election of Chairman and Vice-Chairman

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association is scheduled to hold its first executive committee meeting of the tenth session at 4:00 PM today. They will mutually elect one chairman, one vice-chairman, and three standing committee members. They will also discuss the following important matters entrusted by the first representative assembly: (1) The Municipal Council's collection of municipal general taxes should not be based on valuation except for self-produced and self-used goods; (2) Reducing peddler license fees and addressing cases of abusive treatment of peddlers by patrolmen; and (3) The Municipal Council should provide advance notice when collecting municipal general taxes to avoid complications. Also, the matter of organizing a porter group by the national goods market and requesting exemption from license fees. The association notified all executive committee members yesterday to attend the meeting on time.

Partial Resumption of Work in Customs Brokerage Industry Today

▲ Yarn Industry Allowed to Continue Paying Transportation Fees

▲ Cotton Cloth Industry Still Insisting, No Decision Yet

After the strike of workers in the customs brokerage industry in this city, the transportation of cotton cloth and yarn was completely suspended. Yesterday, the Social Affairs Bureau convened a mediation, but no results were achieved. Today, a part of the industry will resume work first, restoring the transportation of cotton yarn. The details of the situation are recorded below:

▲ Union Meeting The Customs Brokerage Industry Union held a meeting of directors and supervisors at 8:00 PM yesterday. Fourteen people, including Ren Xinxiang, attended. Chairman Sun Dongsheng first reported on the progress of the mediation meeting attended at the Social Affairs Bureau. It was resolved that (1) the transportation fees for cotton yarn, etc., will continue to be paid by the Cotton Yarn Industry Association, so work will be resumed first today (the 14th); (2) if the goal is not achieved for cotton cloth, work will not be resumed; (3) the inspection team will continue to depart as usual.

▲ Instruction to the Union The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau issued an instruction to the Customs Brokerage Industry Union yesterday, stating: "In order to comply with the matter, this bureau has investigated that the union declared in the newspaper on behalf of the cotton cloth industry that the freight fees for the union members' transportation would be handled by the buyers themselves. It was alleged that these freight fees could not be guaranteed. As a result, a strike was launched on the 6th of this month, involving the yarn industry as well. Now, it has been found that the cotton yarn industry companies have not deferred the freight fees for the transportation to the buyers. The union should order the members of the cotton yarn department to resume work first on a specific date to distinguish between the two industries. In addition to ordering the Cotton Yarn Industry Association to handle the payment of freight fees as before, this order is urgently issued to the union to comply without violation. Sincerely."

▲ Order to Cotton Yarn Industry The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau issued an order to the Cotton Yarn Industry Association yesterday, stating: "In order to comply with the matter, this bureau has investigated that the cotton cloth industry declared in the newspaper that the freight fees for the transportation would be handled by the buyers themselves, causing a strike by customs brokerage workers, involving this industry as well. Now, it has been found that this industry has not deferred the freight fees for the transportation to the buyers. The union should be ordered to resume work for this industry first. In addition to issuing separate orders, this order is hereby issued to the association to comply. This order."

▲ Mediation Situation At 1:00 PM yesterday, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau convened a formal mediation. Su Houxin and Ren Xinxiang of the Customs Brokerage Industry Union, Chen Songyuan and Shi Zhong'an of the Cotton Cloth Industry Association, and Shi Zhikun of the Customs Brokerage Industry Union attended. Chairman Guo Yongxi and Recorder Wang Zhiqin presided over the meeting. After a long discussion, it was deemed that the content of this case was complex and needed to be considered. The meeting was temporarily adjourned, and mediation will be conducted later.

Jiangsu Province Regularly Holds

Higher General Qualification Examination

▲ County Government Received Letter from Provincial Examination Committee Yesterday

The Jiangsu Provincial Higher General Qualification Examination Committee, after being certified by the Examination Yuan, requires the people of various counties in the province who have equivalent academic qualifications to graduates of secondary or higher schools to take the general qualification examination. Those with equivalent academic qualifications to graduates of universities or specialized schools may take the higher qualification examination. Yesterday, a letter was sent to the Shanghai County Government stating that the registration period for the two qualification examinations has been set from April 17th to May 10th, and May 17th has been set as the start date for the higher examination, and May 30th as the start date for the general examination. They are hereby requested to investigate and inform the personnel within the county who aspire to take the examination. The letter reads: "Respectfully, in accordance with the previously received assignment certificate and qualification examination regulations forwarded by the Examination Yuan, the committee has appointed members in accordance with the regulations and will hold higher and general qualification examinations within the prescribed time limit. After organizing the committee and convening the first meeting of the two qualification examination committees, it was resolved that the registration period for the two qualification examinations will be from April 10th to May 10th, May 17th will be the start date for the higher qualification examination, and May 30th will be the start date for the general qualification examination. In addition to reporting and distributing the information to the newspapers in Beijing, Shanghai, and Zhenjiang, we are sending you one copy each of the qualification examination regulations and registration instructions. We request that your government investigate and inform the personnel within your jurisdiction who aspire to take the examination. With kind regards, this is addressed to the Shanghai County Government."

Luo Panhui, Director of the Two Railway Bureaus, Assumed Office Yesterday

The newly appointed Director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus, Luo Panhui, held a swearing-in ceremony at 10:00 AM yesterday in the auditorium on the second floor of the bureau. Jian Youwen, a special advisor from the Ministry of Railways, was present to supervise the oath, along with Lai Bao and all the staff of the railway bureau, totaling over one hundred people. Director Luo immediately took the oath of office. After the supervising officer Jian handed over the seal, Luo raised his right hand and read the oath, stating that he swore to uphold Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People and national laws, to be loyal and diligent in his duties, and to never abuse private interests or accept bribes. If he violated the oath, he would be subject to the most severe punishment by the party. Then, the supervising officer Jian Youwen delivered a speech, which was followed by a speech from the former director Liu Weichi, and then a reply from the new director Luo Panhui. After taking a photograph, the ceremony was completed. An announcement was then posted, stating: "Announcement: It is hereby announced that in accordance with Order No. 2338 of the Ministry of Railways on April 9th of this year, Luo Panhui is hereby appointed as the Director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus. This order, etc. Having received this, the director of this bureau followed the order and took office on the 13th of this month. In addition to reporting and distributing the information, this announcement is made to all employees of this railway for their information. This announcement is made on April 13th, the 20th year of the Republic of China. Director Luo Panhui."

Banking Law Does Not Apply to Native Banks

▲ Yarn Industry Sent Letter to Municipal Chamber of Commerce Yesterday

▲ Directly Restricted in Native Banks

▲ Indirectly Affected Among All Industries

The Yarn Industry Association sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating: "Respectfully, according to reports, Article 1 of the Banking Law passed by the Legislative Yuan states that those engaged in one of the following businesses are banks: (1) receiving deposits and making loans; (2) discounting bills; (3) remittance or negotiation of exchange. Those engaged in one of the above businesses but not calling themselves banks are regarded as banks. Although native banks are not explicitly listed, they are included. Banks and native banks are similar in behavior but different in nature. One determines the terms of a transaction based on the collateral and price of the person, while the other determines the standard for making loans based on the brand and credit of the person. One does not speak of sentiment in accordance with the law, while the other prioritizes sentiment and overlooks the law. Therefore, for hundreds of years until recently, those seeking commercial interests only knew whether native banks had resources and did not hear of banks providing emergency relief. For example, our yarn industry, with hundreds of companies in Shanghai, relies on native banks as the hub for business to develop. If the law is used to equate banks with native banks, then how dare the native banks assume unlimited responsibilities with limited financial resources? They will inevitably prioritize the law and disregard the habit of valuing credit and morality that has been cultivated over the years, thereby reducing the scope to pursue meager profits. Native banks will be directly restricted, and all industries will be indirectly affected. This is not to advocate for the financial industry, but it is related to the lifeline of all industries and cannot be kept silent. If this law is implemented without modification, the department stores and commercial activities in urban areas and towns will gradually decline, and there will be an unbearable day. All of our colleagues are uneasy. Considering that your association is the leader of the merchants and all members are well-versed in commercial conditions, they must have the same thoughts and feelings. They will surely report the situation and request instructions to protect all industries and revitalize the market. We hereby request that your association investigate and promptly submit the report to the Yuan, the Ministry, and the Municipal Government for review and implementation. With kind regards, etc."

Japanese Inspection Group Arrives in Shanghai

▲ Over a Thousand Japanese Merchants Tour the City Yesterday

▲ Japanese Residents Hold a Large Banquet at the New World Restaurant

▲ Today to Suzhou and Hangzhou, Friday to Qingdao

The Japanese Tokai Chamber of Commerce and Industry Federation's Chinese inspection group of over a thousand people, led by Ito Jirozaemon, President of the Nagoya Chamber of Commerce and Industry, Kanno Saburo, President of the Toyohashi Chamber of Commerce, Chiga Sentaro, President of the Okazaki Chamber of Commerce, Nishida, Vice President of the Otsu Chamber of Commerce, Danda Kahe, Vice President of the Ogaki Chamber of Commerce, and Sato Soroku, Vice President of the Gifu Chamber of Commerce, arrived in Shanghai at 11:00 AM yesterday on the new ship "Kinnillo" of the Osaka Shosen Kaisha. They landed at the Yangshupu Wharf and boarded 250 cars, divided into three groups: Dongya, New World, and Datong. Students from the Toa Dobun Shoin served as guides and visited various places in the city. In the evening, Mitsui & Co., Sumitomo Bank, Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and Industry, Bank of Chosen, Japan Cotton Trading Co., Mitsubishi Bank, Osaka Shosen Branch, Japan Textile Industry Association, Mitsui Bank, Bank of Taiwan, Osaka Trade Research Institute, Shanghai Trade Research Institute, and Ito & Co. hosted a banquet at the New World Restaurant. The ballroom of the restaurant was temporarily closed for one day for the large-scale banquet. Due to the large number of cars, there was no place to park, so the restaurant applied to the Municipal Council to temporarily borrow the racecourse as a temporary parking lot. After the banquet, the group returned to the ship to stay overnight. Today, they will travel to Suzhou and Hangzhou for sightseeing. This Friday, they will leave Shanghai on the original ship to inspect Qingdao and then return to Osaka.
